 The present Saharanpur district jail used to be the fort of Rohilla dynasty about 200 years ago
 lekin, san 1868 main is mahal ko jail bana diya gaya
 The jail had a capacity of 232 inmates at that time
 varsh 1920 main bhartiya puraatatv vibhaag ne is jail ko sangrakshit smarak ghoshit kar diya

 varsh 2014 main puraatatv vibhaag ne jail ke kuch hisson main khodai kii thi

 jail ke get par ab bhi pathar laga he, jisamen rohilla vansh ke bare main jaankaree likhi he

 haalanki, isaki kshamta 530 ke mukaable philvakt jail main 1690 bandi / kaidi band hai

 bijepi ne chunaav ayog, centre sarkaar or sensor board ko chitthee bhi likhi
 Said that this film can hurt the sentiments of the Kshatriya community
 lihaaja film ko relies se pehle party ke rajput pratinidhiyon ko dikhaaya janaa chahie
 The party argues that by doing this, the film will be convenient for the release and any kind of stressful situations will be avoided
 kai netaa kar chuke hai film kaa viroofilm kaa virodh sirf bijepi hi nahin congress or duusare dalon ne bhi kii he
 The BJP has opposed this by leaders like Union Ministers Uma Bharti, Anil Vij and Sakshi Maharaj
 gujarat ke purv mukhyamantri or rajput netaa shankar singh waghela ne bhi film kii relies kaa virodh kiya he
 Deepika Padukone is playing the role of Padmavati in Scramble with Bhansali
 jabaki allaudin khilji ke kirdaar main ranvir singh hai
 Karni Sena has been opposing this since the shooting of the film
 rajasthan main shooting ke vakt todphod kii ghatana hui thi
 Karani Sena workers also had a scuffle with the film's director Sanjay Leela Bhansali
 safai de chuke hai bhansalibta den ki padmavati main allaudin khilji or rani padmini ke bich dream sikvence ko lekar vivaad tha jis par mekars kii ore se safai aa chuki he
 Bhansali recently said once again on social media that there is no such sequence in the film
 ye film 1 disambar ko relies honi he

 Interesting history on Barwala seat of Haryana: MLA never won again MLA: Haryana has many seats in the assembly elections that have consistently held records and are known for their old history
 is baar ke vidhansabha chunaav ke nateezon par sab kii najar is baat par he ki kya ye aitihaasik vidhansabha siten apane itihaas ko badal paaengi yaa phir puraani parampara kaayam rahegi
 The history of Barwala assembly seat in Hisar district of Haryana is quite interesting
 is seat se ek baar banane vaale vidhayak dobaaraa se kabhi vidhansabha nahin pahunch sake hai
 Not only this, political parties also refrain from fielding a winning candidate again
 iske baavjood agar vah tikat paane main kisi tarah se safal rah jate hai to janata unhen nakaar detii he
 The result of this is that the MLA, once won from Barwala, could not see the face of the assembly again
 barwaala vidhansabha seat kya is baar bhi apane itihaas ko doharayegi?vidhayak veda naarang ne apni partyindian neshnal lokdal main hue bikharavaur chautaala parivaar kii tut se dukhi hokar is baar chunaav ladane se inkaar kar diya
 For this reason, this time all the new faces are in the fray for Barwala assembly seat
 is baar ke vidhansabha chunaav main barwaala seat par jabardast muqabla he
 Ramnivas Dhadola, who is contesting as an Independent from Barwala, said that after winning the election several times, he becomes proud after becoming an MLA and has no concern with the public
 isi vajah se janata bhi aise vidhayak ko dobaaraa vot nahin detii or yahi barwaala kaa itihaas bhi rahaa he
 At the same time, Congress candidate Bhupendra Gangwane said that the public will answer this question as to why she does not choose the MLA once elected
 lekin agar aap janata ke kaam nahin karenge to unase vot kii ummid bhi kaise kar sakate hai
 bjp's candidate Surendra Poonia is claiming his victory
 haalanki wo barwaala kii janata ke mizaaj ko lekar kuch bhi nahin bol rahe hai
 The people of Barwala say that the MLA who won the election once again started walking in long trains and did not have any concern with the public
 isi vajah se janata har chunaav main kisi bhi vidhayak ko dobaaraa se nahin chunati he
 The public trusts the same candidate who is directly connected to them, but ironically, once the MLA is elected, that leader is not able to directly connect with the public, that is why the public rejects that leader in the next election
 karmchaaree rajya beemaa nigam, karnataka main senior resident ke pad par vaikency hai
 Interested candidates can give the interview on 15 April 2015
 pad kaa naam:senior residentpadon kii sankhya:11yogyata:manyata praapt santhaan se embibies

 According to experts, Asaram Bapu has done this trick due to the upcoming Lok Sabha elections
 kyonki asaram baapu ko pataa he ki chunaav ke thik pehle agar rajasthan sarkaar kisi bhi tarah kii riyaayat dene kaa man banaati he to vah or unke samarthak bhaajapa ke saath khadey ho jaaenge or iskaa sidhaa phayda chunaav main milegaa
 In this case, the father of the victim girl in Shahjahanpur said that Asaram Bapu's trick is to get the government to lure votes
 kyonki agar rajasthan sarkaar asaram baapu ke paksh main koi kadam uthaati he to asaram baapu ke lakhon samarthak sarkaar ke liye naram ho jaaenge or iskaa phayda chunaav ke dauraan milane kii sambhaavna bad jaaegi
 The victim's father also said that if this happens then it would be very wrong
 peedita ke pita ne kaha ki asaram baapu ek shaitan hai jise kisi bhi tareeke kii riyaayat nahin milani chahie
 The father said that he had full faith in the law and hoped that the victim girl would get complete justice
 philhal is maamle main rajasthan sarkaar kii taraf se koi bhi aadhikarik bayaan nahin aayaa he lekin sutara bataate hai ki sarkaar sari sthitiyon ko samaj kar hi koi kadam uthaane ke paksh main hai
 Let me tell you that the 16-year-old victim had said in her complaint that Asaram called her to her ashram in Manai area of jodhpur on the night of August 5, 2013 and raped her
 peedita upi ke shahjahanpur se taalluk rakhti he or asaram ke madhya pradesh ke chhindwara sthit ashram main padhati thi
